Even though a dinner of this quality is complimentary, it really detracts from the points of a five-star hotel. Giving gifts is a good thing, but this kind of gift is not as good as giving away.
Second, the hotel's elevators, four elevators are supposed to cover more than 20 floors, so it shouldn't be a problem. Maybe the elevator is too old and slow, and the computer chip is a bit stupid and has low intelligence. As a result, this was the first time I encountered a crowded elevator in a five-star hotel and the elevator was full.
Third, the hotel has a refrigerator, but it is empty. Four bottles of mineral water were given as a gift. This is not Africa. Do we need so much mineral water? Nowadays, many budget business hotels will put a Coke and Sprite as a gift as long as they have a refrigerator. Ordinarily, the cost of Coke is now about the same as that of mineral water. Can't you use dim sum, be more differentiated and diversified? Are you still stuck in the business and management ideas in the early days of reform and opening up?
The hotel's breakfast buffet is in the Western restaurant, and the quality is obviously much higher than the dinner buffet. Although there are a lot of diners, at least there is room to fight.
The hotel has a strategic location, just across the road from Wanda Plaza, diagonally across from the museum and cultural center, and within walking distance of Huiyue Darong City.
The parking lot is large, and parking can be found in the front and back yards. Guests can scan the QR code and enter their car number when leaving the hotel, and parking is free.
